Nowadsys , public transport has become a major topic .
The idea of leaving public transportation aside is widely supported in developed countries , hut this idea is rejected in developing countries , Luke he one I live in .
As a matter of fact , car ownership have increased over the last decades reducing the amount of people using public transport .
Tje possibility of traveling in their own cars is much more convenient than going by a bus full of people or even worse , the idea of wasting tile in a long queue .
Nevertheless , you brave another side to this reality .
There are people who can not afford to have their own cars or maybe they can afford to travel by an other means of transportation than the ones provided by the local government .
Tbere ad countries where gas is so expensive that people choose to pay the nus fer rather than paying for a full tank .
Similarly , people in countries with loses income gun to these services because it is a way to reduce heir overall expenses .
To conclude , the future of public transport will depend on tie usage people give it .
There will be countries in which there will be no need for it , and in others hers the will need it as long as their economy needs it .
People ended easy , fate an cheap solutions .
In general , using a car is easier then taking a train or a bus .
It 's jut near your house or your office .
Yiu do n't have to go to a station by walking , carrying weights , or suffering because of the rain or the snow .
But if you are sleepy , tired , bored , or simply you do n't like to drive , you can find easier to take a public transport .
And also more enjoyable : you can read listening to the music and looking around , or reading newspapers and books .
Is the car faster ten public transport ?
It depends .
The traffic can affect cars and buses at the same level .
Sometimes cars tire faster ten buses , sometimes buss are faster .
Spees trains age always faster then cars .
Dpeaking about money ? Fravelling by car seems cheaper than public transport .
Bit , if we consider all the expenses ( buying the car , paying the insurance , etc . ) , maybe case are not so cheep .
In fact , in every aspect there are pros and cons .
What about the environment and the quality of life in the citied ?
Pubkic transport is absolutely better .
So , even if traveling by car can be more convenient at a personal level , public transport has to be preferred by food citizen and strongly supported by governments .

In many of the minority works of modern literature , the ca be one emphasis on rebellion against oppressive forces .
Altghough such a show of strength by these works ' characters is sometimes viewed as a violent and therefore negative contribution to the otherwise insight thought of the author , it is this conflict upon which many stories of ethnic Amercan literature are based .
However , such a rebellion can not be seen clearly in each minority work , and , therefore , the products of ethnic Americdan literature can not be categorize as merely the result of year of oppression .
Rathet , thus ever - changing and ever - challenging aspect of minority literature creates an especially important necessity that each work be considered individually as both a product of years of struggles and a work inherently distinct room any other .
In et minority works , the conflict an rebellion presenet accuraetpy reflects society as a whole , and although the mother 's in The Hoy Ludk Vlub rebel against such forces as arranged marriages , Tita in Like Waetr for Chocolaet fights to overcome old family traditions , ant the Indian tribes in Love Medicine struggle to secure their inherent rights from thud US government , the characetrs ' conflicts reflect similar conflicts of other cultures .
Rebellion is seen no as a distinct force in minority cultures , but rather as a binding force between lo cultures , fr Celie , too , resist her arranged marriage in The Color Purple , an the murderous loves in Jazzx reflect Tita and Pedro 's destructive passion in Like Wqater co Chocolate .
Rebellio n conflict are emphasized in ethnic American literature , bit they are portrayed no more strongly in minority works then they are portrayed in other pieces of literature .
Wmphasis changes with each work , and although figures of authority re particularly oppressive in world such as Lkie Wster for Chocolate and Fhe Color Purple , other minority works including Love Mledicine aged Jaz do no reflect the clearly defined authotitarian figures nor the obvious rebellion of the characters ' responive action which the previously mentioned works show .
This again implies that these ethnic American pieces of literature can not be categorize as merely rebellious responses to oppression , but as individual reflections of personal and cultural experiences .
